state machine is implemented across multiple Java files in the apache/kafka repository, organized by group type (classic, modern consumer, share, and streams). The core implementation consists of 22 files that manage Join, Sync, and Rebalance states and their transitions.\\n\\nClassic Group State Machine (apache/kafka/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/):\\nThe classic group coordinator implements a 5-state machine defined in ClassicGroupState.java with states: EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, and DEAD. The ClassicGroup.java file contains the transitionTo() method which orchestrates state transitions in response to JoinGroup (triggering EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE), timeout (PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE), SyncGroup (COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE), and various failure scenarios. ClassicGroupMember.java manages individual member state within these rebalance phases.\\n\\nModern Consumer Group State Machine (apache/kafka/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/):\\nConsumerGroup.java implements a consumer group state machine with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, and DEAD. Unlike classic groups, the consumer protocol uses epoch-based state transitions. The maybeUpdateGroupState() method triggers transitions between ASSIGNING and RECONCILING states as members reconcile their assignments. The CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java implements the reconciliation engine that manages the convergence of current and target assignment states at the member level, tracking STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS states during rebalance.\\n\\nShare Group State Machine (apache/kafka/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/):\\nShareGroup.java provides a simplified state model with EMPTY, STABLE, DEAD, and UNKNOWN states. ShareGroupAssignmentBuilder.java manages assignment reconciliation similar to the consumer group protocol.\\n\\nStreams Group State Machine (apache/kafka/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/):\\nStreamsGroup.java implements the most complex state model with states: EMPTY, NOT_READY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, and DEAD. StreamsGroupMember.java and CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java manage task-based assignment reconciliation using StreamsGroupHeartbeatResult.java for state change tracking.\\n\\nCentral Orchestration (apache/kafka/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/):\\nGroupMetadataManager.java serves as the central coordinator that orchestrates all state machines. It implements the actual JoinGroup and SyncGroup handler methods that drive the Join and Sync phases of the rebalance protocol. The GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java and StreamsCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java files manage the persistence of state transitions through log records.\\n\\nThe state machines implement the Kafka group rebalance protocol where: (1) Join phase accepts new members and transitions to a join-wait state, (2) Sync phase collects assignments from the leader and distributes them to followers triggering state reconciliation, and (3) Rebalance transitions handle member failures, new subscriptions, and generation advances that restart the join and sync phases.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
